              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-a1a835d6-e109-47cb-8f03-3c19d4f0333d');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

      "source": [
        "#all players are here with all attrib and age added\n",
        "unique_players = pd.read_sql(\"\"\"SELECT \tplayer_name, PLAYER.player_api_id as player_id,\n",
        "                                        PA_Grouped.date AS date, birthday,\n",
        "                                        AVG(weight) AS avg_weight,\n",
        "                                        AVG(height) AS avg_height,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_overall_rating)) AS avg_overall_rating,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_potential)) AS avg_potential,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_crossing)) AS avg_crossing,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_finishing)) AS avg_finishing,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_heading_accuracy)) AS avg_heading_accuracy,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_short_passing)) AS avg_short_passing,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_dribbling)) AS avg_dribbling,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_free_kick_accuracy)) AS avg_free_kick_accuracy,\n",
        "                                        (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_long_passing)) AS avg_long_passing,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_ball_control)) AS avg_ball_control,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_shot_power)) AS avg_shot_power,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_stamina)) AS avg_stamina,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_strength)) AS avg_strength,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_positioning)) AS avg_positioning,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_vision)) AS avg_vision,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_penalties)) AS avg_penalties,\n",
        "                                       (avg(PA_Grouped.avg_gk_reflexes)) AS avg_gk_reflexes\n",
        "                            FROM PLAYER\n",
        "                            LEFT JOIN (SELECT Player_Attributes.player_api_id,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.overall_rating) AS avg_overall_rating,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.potential) AS avg_potential,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.crossing) AS avg_crossing,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.finishing) AS avg_finishing,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.heading_accuracy) AS avg_heading_accuracy,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.short_passing) AS avg_short_passing,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.dribbling) AS avg_dribbling,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.free_kick_accuracy) AS avg_free_kick_accuracy,\n",
        "                                        avg(Player_Attributes.long_passing) AS avg_long_passing,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.ball_control) AS avg_ball_control,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.shot_power) AS avg_shot_power,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.stamina) AS avg_stamina,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.strength) AS avg_strength,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.positioning) AS avg_positioning,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.vision) AS avg_vision,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.penalties) AS avg_penalties,\n",
        "                                       avg(Player_Attributes.gk_reflexes) AS avg_gk_reflexes,\n",
        "                                       date\n",
        "                                       FROM Player_Attributes\n",
        "                                       GROUP BY Player_Attributes.player_api_id)\n",
        "                                       AS PA_Grouped ON PLAYER.player_api_id = PA_Grouped.player_api_id\n",
        "                            GROUP BY PLAYER.player_api_id\n",
        "                            ORDER BY PLAYER.player_api_id;\"\"\", conn)\n",
        "unique_players.info()"
      ]
    },

        "unique_players[['date','birthday']] = unique_players[['date','birthday']].apply(pd.to_datetime)\n",
        "unique_players['age'] = (unique_players['date'] - unique_players['birthday']).dt.days // 365\n",
        "unique_players['avg_vision'].fillna(unique_players['avg_vision'].mean(), inplace = True)\n",
        "unique_players.info()"

              "    }\n",

              "      const quickchartButtonEl =\n",

            "application/vnd.google.colaboratory.intrinsic+json": {
              "type": "dataframe",
              "variable_name": "best_teams",
              "summary": "{\n  \"name\": \"best_teams\",\n  \"rows\": 295,\n  \"fields\": [\n    {\n      \"column\": \"total_games\",\n      \"properties\": {\n        \"dtype\": \"number\",\n        \"std\": 96,\n        \"min\": 30,\n        \"max\": 304,\n        \"num_unique_values\": 56,\n        \"samples\": [\n          304,\n          303,\n          126\n        ],\n        \"semantic_type\": \"\",\n        \"description\": \"\"\n      }\n    },\n    {\n      \"column\": \"team_name\",\n      \"properties\": {\n        \"dtype\": \"string\",\n        \"num_unique_values\": 295,\n        \"samples\": [\n          \"Cardiff City\",\n          \"KVC Westerlo\",\n          \"Ruch Chorz\\u00f3w\"\n        ],\n        \"semantic_type\": \"\",\n        \"description\": \"\"\n      }\n    },\n    {\n      \"column\": \"wins\",\n      \"properties\": {\n        \"dtype\": \"number\",\n        \"std\": 51,\n        \"min\": 3,\n        \"max\": 234,\n        \"num_unique_values\": 133,\n        \"samples\": [\n          99,\n          78,\n          127\n        ],\n        \"semantic_type\": \"\",\n        \"description\": \"\"\n      }\n    },\n    {\n      \"column\": \"win_percentage\",\n      \"properties\": {\n        \"dtype\": \"number\",\n        \"std\": 12,\n        \"min\": 7,\n        \"max\": 76,\n        \"num_unique_values\": 60,\n        \"samples\": [\n          76,\n          62,\n          32\n        ],\n        \"semantic_type\": \"\",\n        \"description\": \"\"\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}"
            }
          },
          "metadata": {},
          "execution_count": 7
        }
      ],
      "source": [
        "#team winning percentage relative to all games\n",
        "\n",
        "best_teams = pd.read_sql(\"\"\"WITH\n",
        "                        temp AS (\n",
        "\n",
        "                            SELECT m.match_api_id,\n",
        "                                ht.team_long_name AS  home_team,\n",
        "                                AT.team_long_name AS away_team,\n",
        "                                home_team_goal,\n",
        "                                away_team_goal,\n",
        "                                ht.team_api_id AS h_id,\n",
        "                                at.team_api_id AS a_id,\n",
        "                            CASE\n",
        "                                when m.home_team_goal > m.away_team_goal then ht.team_api_id\n",
        "                                when m.home_team_goal < m.away_team_goal then at.team_api_id else 'Draw' end as winner\n",
        "                            FROM Match AS m\n",
        "                            LEFT JOIN Team AS ht on ht.team_api_id = m.home_team_api_id\n",
        "                            LEFT JOIN Team AS at on at.team_api_id = m.away_team_api_id\n",
        "                        ),\n",
        "                        home AS (\n",
        "                            SELECT COUNT(match_api_id) AS home_games,\n",
        "                                home_team AS team_name,\n",
        "                                h_id\n",
        "                            FROM temp\n",
        "                            GROUP BY home_team\n",
        "                        ),\n",
        "                        away AS (\n",
        "                            SELECT COUNT(match_api_id) AS away_games,\n",
        "                                away_team AS team_name,\n",
        "                                a_id\n",
        "                            FROM temp\n",
        "                            GROUP BY away_team\n",
        "                        ),\n",
        "                        total AS (\n",
        "                            SELECT a.away_games + h.home_games AS total_games,\n",
        "                            h.team_name,\n",
        "                            h.h_id\n",
        "                            FROM home AS h\n",
        "                            JOIN away AS a ON h.h_id = a.a_id\n",
        "                            GROUP BY h.team_name\n",
        "                        ),\n",
        "                        wins AS (\n",
        "                            SELECT winner, COUNT(*) AS wins\n",
        "                            FROM temp\n",
        "                            GROUP BY winner\n",
        "                        )\n",
        "\n",
        "                        SELECT t.total_games,\n",
        "                            t.team_name,\n",
        "                            w.wins,\n",
        "                            (w.wins)*100/(t.total_games) AS win_percentage\n",
        "                        FROM total AS t\n",
        "                        JOIN wins AS w on t.h_id = w.winner\n",
        "                        ORDER BY wins DESC;\"\"\", conn)\n",
        "best_teams.head(5)"
      ]
    },
    {

        "best_players = pd.read_sql(\"\"\"SELECT pa.player_api_id , p.player_name , pa.overall_rating\n",
        "                FROM Player_Attributes as pa\n",
        "                INNER JOIN Player as p\n",
        "                ON pa.player_api_id = p.player_api_id\n",
        "                GROUP BY pa.player_api_id\n",
        "                ORDER BY pa.overall_rating DESC;\"\"\", conn)\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-ae069eb7-c59d-4ab2-8e6d-d0471e759d55');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

        "#group by away/home goals scored, or by general indicators. Just a cut of the data\n",
        "\n",
        "away_perf = pd.read_sql_query(\"\"\"WITH home AS (\n",
        "    SELECT\n",
        "        home_team_api_id,\n",
        "        t.team_long_name || ' (' || c.name || ')' AS team_name,\n",
        "        SUM(m.home_team_goal) AS home_goal\n",
        "    FROM\n",
        "        match AS m\n",
        "        LEFT JOIN country AS c ON m.country_id = c.id\n",
        "        LEFT JOIN team AS t ON t.team_api_id = m.home_team_api_id\n",
        "    GROUP BY\n",
        "        home_team_api_id, team_name\n",
        "),\n",
        "away AS (\n",
        "    SELECT\n",
        "        away_team_api_id,\n",
        "        t.team_long_name || ' (' || c.name || ')' AS team_name,\n",
        "        SUM(m.away_team_goal) AS away_goal\n",
        "    FROM\n",
        "        match AS m\n",
        "        LEFT JOIN country AS c ON m.country_id = c.id\n",
        "        LEFT JOIN team AS t ON t.team_api_id = m.away_team_api_id\n",
        "    GROUP BY\n",
        "        away_team_api_id, team_name\n",
        ")\n",
        "SELECT\n",
        "    COALESCE(home_team_api_id, away_team_api_id) AS team_api_id,\n",
        "    COALESCE(home.team_name, away.team_name) AS team_name,\n",
        "    COALESCE(away_goal, 0) AS away_goal,\n",
        "    COALESCE(home_goal, 0) AS home_goal,\n",
        "    COALESCE(away_goal, 0) + COALESCE(home_goal, 0) AS total_goal\n",
        "FROM\n",
        "    away\n",
        "    LEFT JOIN home ON home.team_name = away.team_name\n",
        "ORDER BY\n",
        "    total_goal DESC;\"\"\", conn)\n",
        "\n",
        "away_perf"
      ]
    },

        "allmatches = pd.read_sql_query (\"\"\"SELECT\n",
        "    match.match_api_id,\n",
        "    l.name AS league,\n",
        "    l.id AS league_id,\n",
        "    Country.name AS country,\n",
        "    match.season,\n",
        "    match.date,\n",
        "    match.stage,\n",
        "    B365H, B365D, B365A,\n",
        "    CASE\n",
        "        WHEN match.home_team_goal > match.away_team_goal THEN Team.team_long_name\n",
        "        WHEN match.home_team_goal < match.away_team_goal THEN OpponentTeam.team_long_name\n",
        "        ELSE 'Draw'\n",
        "    END AS winner,\n",
        "    Team.team_long_name AS home_team,\n",
        "    Team.team_short_name AS home_team_short,\n",
        "    match.home_team_api_id AS h_api_id,\n",
        "    match.home_team_goal AS home_goal,\n",
        "    CASE\n",
        "        WHEN match.home_team_goal = match.away_team_goal THEN 1\n",
        "        WHEN match.home_team_goal > match.away_team_goal THEN 3\n",
        "        ELSE 0\n",
        "    END AS home_Points,\n",
        "    OpponentTeam.team_long_name AS away_team,\n",
        "    OpponentTeam.team_short_name AS away_team_short,\n",
        "    match.away_team_api_id AS a_api_id,\n",
        "    match.away_team_goal AS away_goal,\n",
        "    CASE\n",
        "        WHEN match.home_team_goal = match.away_team_goal THEN 1\n",
        "        WHEN match.home_team_goal < match.away_team_goal THEN 3\n",
        "        ELSE 0\n",
        "    END AS away_Points,\n",
        "    match.home_team_goal - match.away_team_goal AS goal_dif,\n",
        "    match.home_team_goal + match.away_team_goal AS match_goals\n",
        "FROM\n",
        "    match\n",
        "JOIN\n",
        "    Country ON match.country_id = Country.id\n",
        "JOIN\n",
        "    League AS l ON match.league_id = l.id\n",
        "JOIN\n",
        "    Team ON match.home_team_api_id = Team.team_api_id\n",
        "JOIN\n",
        "    Team AS OpponentTeam ON match.away_team_api_id = OpponentTeam.team_api_id\n",
        "JOIN\n",
        "    Team_Attributes AS htr ON htr.team_api_id = match.home_team_api_id\n",
        "JOIN\n",
        "    Team_Attributes AS atr ON atr.team_api_id = match.away_team_api_id\n",
        "GROUP BY\n",
        "    match.match_api_id;\n",
        "\"\"\", conn)\n",
        "allmatches.info()"
      ]
    },
    {

        "def this_map(x):\n",
        "    if x < 0:\n",
        "        return -1\n",
        "    if x > 0:\n",
        "        return 1\n",
        "    return 0\n",
        "allmatches['result'] = allmatches['home_goal'] - allmatches['away_goal']\n",
        "allmatches['result'] = allmatches['result'].apply(lambda x:this_map(x))\n",
        "\n",
        "allmatches.info()"
      ]

      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "#aggregation team points for Classification models\n",
        "\n",
        "team_points = pd.read_sql(\"\"\"SELECT\n",
        "                                        l.name AS league,\n",
        "                                        t.team_long_name as team_name,\n",
        "                                        t.team_api_id as team_api_id,\n",
        "                                        sum(CASE\n",
        "                                        WHEN home_team_goal = away_team_goal THEN 1\n",
        "                                        WHEN home_team_goal > away_team_goal THEN 3\n",
        "                                        WHEN home_team_goal < away_team_goal THEN 0\n",
        "                                        END)home_Points,\n",
        "                                        sum(CASE\n",
        "                                        WHEN home_team_goal = away_team_goal THEN 1\n",
        "                                        WHEN home_team_goal < away_team_goal THEN 3\n",
        "                                        WHEN home_team_goal > away_team_goal THEN 0\n",
        "                                        END)away_Points\n",
        "                                FROM Match m\n",
        "                                JOIN Country c on c.id = m.country_id\n",
        "                                JOIN League l on l.id = m.league_id\n",
        "                                LEFT JOIN Team AS t on t.team_api_id = m.home_team_api_id\n",
        "                                GROUP BY  t.team_long_name\n",
        "                                ORDER BY  t.team_long_name;\"\"\", conn)\n",
        "team_points.info()"
      ],

      "cell_type": "code",

        "  \t\tavg(Team_Attributes.buildupplaydribbling) as avg_PlayDribbling,\n",
        "  \t\tavg(Team_Attributes.chanceCreationPassing) as avg_CreationPassing,\n",

        "# is it true that teams perform better on home ground???\n",
        "\n",
        "away_home_win = pd.read_sql_query(\"SELECT \\\n",
        "                        c.name,\\\n",
        "                        case when m.home_team_goal > m.away_team_goal Then 'HOME'\\\n",
        "                        when m.home_team_goal < m.away_team_goal Then 'AWAY'\\\n",
        "                        else 'DRAW' end as VENUE,\\\n",
        "                        count(*) as WINS\\\n",
        "                    FROM\\\n",
        "                        Match as m\\\n",
        "                        join Country as c\\\n",
        "                        on c.id = m.country_id\\\n",
        "                    group by c.name, VENUE\\\n",
        "                    order by c.name desc;\"\"\", conn)\n",
        "\n",
        "plt.figure(figsize=(12, 8))\n",
        "sns.barplot(x='name', y='WINS', data=away_home_win, hue='VENUE', palette='Set2')\n",
        "plt.show()"
      ],

    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "from scipy.stats import entropy\n",
        "def match_entropy(row):\n",
        "    odds = [row['B365H'],row['B365D'],row['B365A']]\n",
        "    #change odds to probability\n",
        "    probs = [1/o for o in odds]\n",
        "    #normalize to sum to 1\n",
        "    norm = sum(probs)\n",
        "    probs = [p/norm for p in probs]\n",
        "    return entropy(probs)\n",
        "allmatches['entropy'] = allmatches.apply(match_entropy,axis=1)"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "Xc0zL9MsQ5c4"
      },
      "execution_count": 26,
      "outputs": []
    },

        "entropy_means = entropy_means.reset_index().pivot(index='season', columns='league', values='entropy')\n",
        "entropy_means.head(10)"

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-05f72a09-9525-4da4-9440-e9efe854e965');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "         border-bottom: 1px solid var(--colab-border-color);\"><b>sqlalchemy.engine.create.create_engine</b><br/>def create_engine(url: Union[str, _url.URL], **kwargs: Any) -&gt; Engine</pre><pre class=\"function-repr-contents function-repr-contents-collapsed\" style=\"\"><a class=\"filepath\" style=\"display:none\" href=\"#\">/usr/local/lib/python3.10/dist-packages/sqlalchemy/engine/create.py</a>Create a new :class:`_engine.Engine` instance.\n",
              "\n",
              "The standard calling form is to send the :ref:`URL &lt;database_urls&gt;` as the\n",
              "first positional argument, usually a string\n",
              "that indicates database dialect and connection arguments::\n",
              "\n",
              "    engine = create_engine(&quot;postgresql+psycopg2://scott:tiger@localhost/test&quot;)\n",
              "\n",
              ".. note::\n",
              "\n",
              "    Please review :ref:`database_urls` for general guidelines in composing\n",
              "    URL strings.  In particular, special characters, such as those often\n",
              "    part of passwords, must be URL encoded to be properly parsed.\n",
              "\n",
              "Additional keyword arguments may then follow it which\n",
              "establish various options on the resulting :class:`_engine.Engine`\n",
              "and its underlying :class:`.Dialect` and :class:`_pool.Pool`\n",
              "constructs::\n",
              "\n",
              "    engine = create_engine(&quot;mysql+mysqldb://scott:tiger@hostname/dbname&quot;,\n",
              "                                pool_recycle=3600, echo=True)\n",
              "\n",
              "The string form of the URL is\n",
              "``dialect[+driver]://user:password@host/dbname[?key=value..]``, where\n",
              "``dialect`` is a database name such as ``mysql``, ``oracle``,\n",
              "``postgresql``, etc., and ``driver`` the name of a DBAPI, such as\n",
              "``psycopg2``, ``pyodbc``, ``cx_oracle``, etc.  Alternatively,\n",
              "the URL can be an instance of :class:`~sqlalchemy.engine.url.URL`.\n",
              "\n",
              "``**kwargs`` takes a wide variety of options which are routed\n",
              "towards their appropriate components.  Arguments may be specific to\n",
              "the :class:`_engine.Engine`, the underlying :class:`.Dialect`,\n",
              "as well as the\n",
              ":class:`_pool.Pool`.  Specific dialects also accept keyword arguments that\n",
              "are unique to that dialect.   Here, we describe the parameters\n",
              "that are common to most :func:`_sa.create_engine()` usage.\n",
              "\n",
              "Once established, the newly resulting :class:`_engine.Engine` will\n",
              "request a connection from the underlying :class:`_pool.Pool` once\n",
              ":meth:`_engine.Engine.connect` is called, or a method which depends on it\n",
              "such as :meth:`_engine.Engine.execute` is invoked.   The\n",
              ":class:`_pool.Pool` in turn\n",
              "will establish the first actual DBAPI connection when this request\n",
              "is received.   The :func:`_sa.create_engine` call itself does **not**\n",
              "establish any actual DBAPI connections directly.\n",
              "\n",
              ".. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "    :doc:`/core/engines`\n",
              "\n",
              "    :doc:`/dialects/index`\n",
              "\n",
              "    :ref:`connections_toplevel`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param connect_args: a dictionary of options which will be\n",
              "    passed directly to the DBAPI&#x27;s ``connect()`` method as\n",
              "    additional keyword arguments.  See the example\n",
              "    at :ref:`custom_dbapi_args`.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param creator: a callable which returns a DBAPI connection.\n",
              "    This creation function will be passed to the underlying\n",
              "    connection pool and will be used to create all new database\n",
              "    connections. Usage of this function causes connection\n",
              "    parameters specified in the URL argument to be bypassed.\n",
              "\n",
              "    This hook is not as flexible as the newer\n",
              "    :meth:`_events.DialectEvents.do_connect` hook which allows complete\n",
              "    control over how a connection is made to the database, given the full\n",
              "    set of URL arguments and state beforehand.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :meth:`_events.DialectEvents.do_connect` - event hook that allows\n",
              "        full control over DBAPI connection mechanics.\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`custom_dbapi_args`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param echo=False: if True, the Engine will log all statements\n",
              "    as well as a ``repr()`` of their parameter lists to the default log\n",
              "    handler, which defaults to ``sys.stdout`` for output.   If set to the\n",
              "    string ``&quot;debug&quot;``, result rows will be printed to the standard output\n",
              "    as well. The ``echo`` attribute of ``Engine`` can be modified at any\n",
              "    time to turn logging on and off; direct control of logging is also\n",
              "    available using the standard Python ``logging`` module.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`dbengine_logging` - further detail on how to configure\n",
              "        logging.\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              ":param echo_pool=False: if True, the connection pool will log\n",
              "    informational output such as when connections are invalidated\n",
              "    as well as when connections are recycled to the default log handler,\n",
              "    which defaults to ``sys.stdout`` for output.   If set to the string\n",
              "    ``&quot;debug&quot;``, the logging will include pool checkouts and checkins.\n",
              "    Direct control of logging is also available using the standard Python\n",
              "    ``logging`` module.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`dbengine_logging` - further detail on how to configure\n",
              "        logging.\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              ":param empty_in_strategy:   No longer used; SQLAlchemy now uses\n",
              "    &quot;empty set&quot; behavior for IN in all cases.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. deprecated:: 1.4 The :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.empty_in_strategy` keyword is deprecated, and no longer has any effect.  All IN expressions are now rendered using the &quot;expanding parameter&quot; strategy which renders a set of boundexpressions, or an &quot;empty set&quot; SELECT, at statement executiontime.\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              ":param enable_from_linting: defaults to True.  Will emit a warning\n",
              "    if a given SELECT statement is found to have un-linked FROM elements\n",
              "    which would cause a cartesian product.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionadded:: 1.4\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`change_4737`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param execution_options: Dictionary execution options which will\n",
              "    be applied to all connections.  See\n",
              "    :meth:`~sqlalchemy.engine.Connection.execution_options`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param future: Use the 2.0 style :class:`_engine.Engine` and\n",
              "    :class:`_engine.Connection` API.\n",
              "\n",
              "    As of SQLAlchemy 2.0, this parameter is present for backwards\n",
              "    compatibility only and must remain at its default value of ``True``.\n",
              "\n",
              "    The :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.future` parameter will be\n",
              "    deprecated in a subsequent 2.x release and eventually removed.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionadded:: 1.4\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionchanged:: 2.0 All :class:`_engine.Engine` objects are\n",
              "       &quot;future&quot; style engines and there is no longer a ``future=False``\n",
              "       mode of operation.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`migration_20_toplevel`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param hide_parameters: Boolean, when set to True, SQL statement parameters\n",
              "    will not be displayed in INFO logging nor will they be formatted into\n",
              "    the string representation of :class:`.StatementError` objects.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionadded:: 1.3.8\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`dbengine_logging` - further detail on how to configure\n",
              "        logging.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param implicit_returning=True:  Legacy parameter that may only be set\n",
              "    to True. In SQLAlchemy 2.0, this parameter does nothing. In order to\n",
              "    disable &quot;implicit returning&quot; for statements invoked by the ORM,\n",
              "    configure this on a per-table basis using the\n",
              "    :paramref:`.Table.implicit_returning` parameter.\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              ":param insertmanyvalues_page_size: number of rows to format into an\n",
              " INSERT statement when the statement uses &quot;insertmanyvalues&quot; mode, which is\n",
              " a paged form of bulk insert that is used for many backends when using\n",
              " :term:`executemany` execution typically in conjunction with RETURNING.\n",
              " Defaults to 1000, but may also be subject to dialect-specific limiting\n",
              " factors which may override this value on a per-statement basis.\n",
              "\n",
              " .. versionadded:: 2.0\n",
              "\n",
              " .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "    :ref:`engine_insertmanyvalues`\n",
              "\n",
              "    :ref:`engine_insertmanyvalues_page_size`\n",
              "\n",
              "    :paramref:`_engine.Connection.execution_options.insertmanyvalues_page_size`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param isolation_level: optional string name of an isolation level\n",
              "    which will be set on all new connections unconditionally.\n",
              "    Isolation levels are typically some subset of the string names\n",
              "    ``&quot;SERIALIZABLE&quot;``, ``&quot;REPEATABLE READ&quot;``,\n",
              "    ``&quot;READ COMMITTED&quot;``, ``&quot;READ UNCOMMITTED&quot;`` and ``&quot;AUTOCOMMIT&quot;``\n",
              "    based on backend.\n",
              "\n",
              "    The :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.isolation_level` parameter is\n",
              "    in contrast to the\n",
              "    :paramref:`.Connection.execution_options.isolation_level`\n",
              "    execution option, which may be set on an individual\n",
              "    :class:`.Connection`, as well as the same parameter passed to\n",
              "    :meth:`.Engine.execution_options`, where it may be used to create\n",
              "    multiple engines with different isolation levels that share a common\n",
              "    connection pool and dialect.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionchanged:: 2.0 The\n",
              "       :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.isolation_level`\n",
              "       parameter has been generalized to work on all dialects which support\n",
              "       the concept of isolation level, and is provided as a more succinct,\n",
              "       up front configuration switch in contrast to the execution option\n",
              "       which is more of an ad-hoc programmatic option.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`dbapi_autocommit`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param json_deserializer: for dialects that support the\n",
              "    :class:`_types.JSON`\n",
              "    datatype, this is a Python callable that will convert a JSON string\n",
              "    to a Python object.  By default, the Python ``json.loads`` function is\n",
              "    used.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionchanged:: 1.3.7  The SQLite dialect renamed this from\n",
              "       ``_json_deserializer``.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param json_serializer: for dialects that support the :class:`_types.JSON`\n",
              "    datatype, this is a Python callable that will render a given object\n",
              "    as JSON.   By default, the Python ``json.dumps`` function is used.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionchanged:: 1.3.7  The SQLite dialect renamed this from\n",
              "       ``_json_serializer``.\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              ":param label_length=None: optional integer value which limits\n",
              "    the size of dynamically generated column labels to that many\n",
              "    characters. If less than 6, labels are generated as\n",
              "    &quot;_(counter)&quot;. If ``None``, the value of\n",
              "    ``dialect.max_identifier_length``, which may be affected via the\n",
              "    :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.max_identifier_length` parameter,\n",
              "    is used instead.   The value of\n",
              "    :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.label_length`\n",
              "    may not be larger than that of\n",
              "    :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.max_identfier_length`.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.max_identifier_length`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param logging_name:  String identifier which will be used within\n",
              "    the &quot;name&quot; field of logging records generated within the\n",
              "    &quot;sqlalchemy.engine&quot; logger. Defaults to a hexstring of the\n",
              "    object&#x27;s id.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`dbengine_logging` - further detail on how to configure\n",
              "        logging.\n",
              "\n",
              "        :paramref:`_engine.Connection.execution_options.logging_token`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param max_identifier_length: integer; override the max_identifier_length\n",
              "    determined by the dialect.  if ``None`` or zero, has no effect.  This\n",
              "    is the database&#x27;s configured maximum number of characters that may be\n",
              "    used in a SQL identifier such as a table name, column name, or label\n",
              "    name. All dialects determine this value automatically, however in the\n",
              "    case of a new database version for which this value has changed but\n",
              "    SQLAlchemy&#x27;s dialect has not been adjusted, the value may be passed\n",
              "    here.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionadded:: 1.3.9\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :paramref:`_sa.create_engine.label_length`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param max_overflow=10: the number of connections to allow in\n",
              "    connection pool &quot;overflow&quot;, that is connections that can be\n",
              "    opened above and beyond the pool_size setting, which defaults\n",
              "    to five. this is only used with :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.QueuePool`.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param module=None: reference to a Python module object (the module\n",
              "    itself, not its string name).  Specifies an alternate DBAPI module to\n",
              "    be used by the engine&#x27;s dialect.  Each sub-dialect references a\n",
              "    specific DBAPI which will be imported before first connect.  This\n",
              "    parameter causes the import to be bypassed, and the given module to\n",
              "    be used instead. Can be used for testing of DBAPIs as well as to\n",
              "    inject &quot;mock&quot; DBAPI implementations into the :class:`_engine.Engine`.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param paramstyle=None: The `paramstyle &lt;https://legacy.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0249/#paramstyle&gt;`_\n",
              "    to use when rendering bound parameters.  This style defaults to the\n",
              "    one recommended by the DBAPI itself, which is retrieved from the\n",
              "    ``.paramstyle`` attribute of the DBAPI.  However, most DBAPIs accept\n",
              "    more than one paramstyle, and in particular it may be desirable\n",
              "    to change a &quot;named&quot; paramstyle into a &quot;positional&quot; one, or vice versa.\n",
              "    When this attribute is passed, it should be one of the values\n",
              "    ``&quot;qmark&quot;``, ``&quot;numeric&quot;``, ``&quot;named&quot;``, ``&quot;format&quot;`` or\n",
              "    ``&quot;pyformat&quot;``, and should correspond to a parameter style known\n",
              "    to be supported by the DBAPI in use.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool=None: an already-constructed instance of\n",
              "    :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.Pool`, such as a\n",
              "    :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.QueuePool` instance. If non-None, this\n",
              "    pool will be used directly as the underlying connection pool\n",
              "    for the engine, bypassing whatever connection parameters are\n",
              "    present in the URL argument. For information on constructing\n",
              "    connection pools manually, see :ref:`pooling_toplevel`.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param poolclass=None: a :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.Pool`\n",
              "    subclass, which will be used to create a connection pool\n",
              "    instance using the connection parameters given in the URL. Note\n",
              "    this differs from ``pool`` in that you don&#x27;t actually\n",
              "    instantiate the pool in this case, you just indicate what type\n",
              "    of pool to be used.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_logging_name:  String identifier which will be used within\n",
              "   the &quot;name&quot; field of logging records generated within the\n",
              "   &quot;sqlalchemy.pool&quot; logger. Defaults to a hexstring of the object&#x27;s\n",
              "   id.\n",
              "\n",
              "   .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`dbengine_logging` - further detail on how to configure\n",
              "        logging.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_pre_ping: boolean, if True will enable the connection pool\n",
              "    &quot;pre-ping&quot; feature that tests connections for liveness upon\n",
              "    each checkout.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionadded:: 1.2\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`pool_disconnects_pessimistic`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_size=5: the number of connections to keep open\n",
              "    inside the connection pool. This used with\n",
              "    :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.QueuePool` as\n",
              "    well as :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.SingletonThreadPool`.  With\n",
              "    :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.QueuePool`, a ``pool_size`` setting\n",
              "    of 0 indicates no limit; to disable pooling, set ``poolclass`` to\n",
              "    :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.NullPool` instead.\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_recycle=-1: this setting causes the pool to recycle\n",
              "    connections after the given number of seconds has passed. It\n",
              "    defaults to -1, or no timeout. For example, setting to 3600\n",
              "    means connections will be recycled after one hour. Note that\n",
              "    MySQL in particular will disconnect automatically if no\n",
              "    activity is detected on a connection for eight hours (although\n",
              "    this is configurable with the MySQLDB connection itself and the\n",
              "    server configuration as well).\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`pool_setting_recycle`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_reset_on_return=&#x27;rollback&#x27;: set the\n",
              "    :paramref:`_pool.Pool.reset_on_return` parameter of the underlying\n",
              "    :class:`_pool.Pool` object, which can be set to the values\n",
              "    ``&quot;rollback&quot;``, ``&quot;commit&quot;``, or ``None``.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`pool_reset_on_return`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_timeout=30: number of seconds to wait before giving\n",
              "    up on getting a connection from the pool. This is only used\n",
              "    with :class:`~sqlalchemy.pool.QueuePool`. This can be a float but is\n",
              "    subject to the limitations of Python time functions which may not be\n",
              "    reliable in the tens of milliseconds.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. note: don&#x27;t use 30.0 above, it seems to break with the :param tag\n",
              "\n",
              ":param pool_use_lifo=False: use LIFO (last-in-first-out) when retrieving\n",
              "    connections from :class:`.QueuePool` instead of FIFO\n",
              "    (first-in-first-out). Using LIFO, a server-side timeout scheme can\n",
              "    reduce the number of connections used during non- peak   periods of\n",
              "    use.   When planning for server-side timeouts, ensure that a recycle or\n",
              "    pre-ping strategy is in use to gracefully   handle stale connections.\n",
              "\n",
              "      .. versionadded:: 1.3\n",
              "\n",
              "      .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`pool_use_lifo`\n",
              "\n",
              "        :ref:`pool_disconnects`\n",
              "\n",
              ":param plugins: string list of plugin names to load.  See\n",
              "    :class:`.CreateEnginePlugin` for background.\n",
              "\n",
              "    .. versionadded:: 1.2.3\n",
              "\n",
              ":param query_cache_size: size of the cache used to cache the SQL string\n",
              " form of queries.  Set to zero to disable caching.\n",
              "\n",
              " The cache is pruned of its least recently used items when its size reaches\n",
              " N * 1.5.  Defaults to 500, meaning the cache will always store at least\n",
              " 500 SQL statements when filled, and will grow up to 750 items at which\n",
              " point it is pruned back down to 500 by removing the 250 least recently\n",
              " used items.\n",
              "\n",
              " Caching is accomplished on a per-statement basis by generating a\n",
              " cache key that represents the statement&#x27;s structure, then generating\n",
              " string SQL for the current dialect only if that key is not present\n",
              " in the cache.   All statements support caching, however some features\n",
              " such as an INSERT with a large set of parameters will intentionally\n",
              " bypass the cache.   SQL logging will indicate statistics for each\n",
              " statement whether or not it were pull from the cache.\n",
              "\n",
              " .. note:: some ORM functions related to unit-of-work persistence as well\n",
              "    as some attribute loading strategies will make use of individual\n",
              "    per-mapper caches outside of the main cache.\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              " .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "    :ref:`sql_caching`\n",
              "\n",
              " .. versionadded:: 1.4\n",
              "\n",
              ":param use_insertmanyvalues: True by default, use the &quot;insertmanyvalues&quot;\n",
              " execution style for INSERT..RETURNING statements by default.\n",
              "\n",
              " .. versionadded:: 2.0\n",
              "\n",
              " .. seealso::\n",
              "\n",
              "    :ref:`engine_insertmanyvalues`</pre>\n",
              "      <script>\n",
              "      if (google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed && google.colab.files && google.colab.files.view) {\n",
